I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
CiliumNetworkingSpec should have a parameter to set Cilium's enable-host-firewall option
/kind feature

**1. Describe IN DETAIL the feature/behavior/change you would like to see.**

There is currently no parameter in [CiliumNetworkingSpec](https://pkg.go.dev/k8s.io/kops/pkg/apis/kops#CiliumNetworkingSpec) that would be used to set the `enable-host-firewall` key in the `cilium-config` ConfigMap or the `--enable-host-firewall` command line argument.

Since kops cannot set it, the cluster operator is required to either edit the ConfigMap manually or manage it using something like ArgoCD, which is somewhat awkward and more prone to human error, as opposed to when it is managed by kops, like it is supposed to be.


**2. Feel free to provide a design supporting your feature request.**

The possible implementation does not seem different from any other boolean parameter.

</pr_description>

    20	        "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/api/resource"
    21	
    22	        "k8s.io/kops/pkg/apis/kops"
    23	        "k8s.io/kops/pkg/wellknownports"
    24	        "k8s.io/kops/upup/pkg/fi"
    25	        "k8s.io/kops/upup/pkg/fi/loader"
    26	)
    27	
    28	// CiliumOptionsBuilder adds options for the cilium to the model
    29	type CiliumOptionsBuilder struct {
    30	        Context *OptionsContext
    31	}
    32	
    33	var _ loader.ClusterOptionsBuilder = &CiliumOptionsBuilder{}
    34	
    35	func (b *CiliumOptionsBuilder) BuildOptions(o *kops.Cluster) error {
    36	        clusterSpec := &o.Spec
    37	        c := clusterSpec.Networking.Cilium
    38	        if c == nil {
    39	                return nil
    40	        }
    41	
    42	        if c.Version == "" {
    43	                c.Version = "v1.18.6"
    44	        }
    45	
    46	        if c.EnableEndpointHealthChecking == nil {
    47	                c.EnableEndpointHealthChecking = fi.PtrTo(true)
    48	        }
    49	
    50	        if c.IdentityAllocationMode == "" {
    51	                c.IdentityAllocationMode = "crd"
    52	        }
    53	
    54	        if c.IdentityChangeGracePeriod == "" {
    55	                c.IdentityChangeGracePeriod = "5s"
    56	        }
    57	
    58	        if c.BPFCTGlobalAnyMax == 0 {
    59	                c.BPFCTGlobalAnyMax = 262144
    60	        }
    61	
    62	        if c.BPFCTGlobalTCPMax == 0 {
    63	                c.BPFCTGlobalTCPMax = 524288
    64	        }
    65	
    66	        if c.BPFLBAlgorithm == "" {
    67	                c.BPFLBAlgorithm = "random"
    68	        }
    69	
    70	        if c.BPFLBMaglevTableSize == "" {
    71	                c.BPFLBMaglevTableSize = "16381"
    72	        }
    73	
    74	        if c.BPFNATGlobalMax == 0 {
    75	                c.BPFNATGlobalMax = 524288
    76	        }
    77	
    78	        if c.BPFNeighGlobalMax == 0 {
    79	                c.BPFNeighGlobalMax = 524288
    80	        }
    81	
    82	        if c.BPFPolicyMapMax == 0 {
    83	                c.BPFPolicyMapMax = 16384
    84	        }
    85	
    86	        if c.BPFLBMapMax == 0 {
    87	                c.BPFLBMapMax = 65536
    88	        }
    89	
    90	        if c.ClusterName == "" {
    91	                c.ClusterName = "default"
    92	        }
    93	
    94	        if c.MonitorAggregation == "" {
    95	                c.MonitorAggregation = "medium"
    96	        }
    97	
    98	        if c.SidecarIstioProxyImage == "" {
    99	                c.SidecarIstioProxyImage = "cilium/istio_proxy"
   100	        }
   101	
   102	        if c.ToFQDNsDNSRejectResponseCode == "" {
   103	                c.ToFQDNsDNSRejectResponseCode = "refused"
   104	        }
   105	
   106	        if c.AgentPrometheusPort == 0 {
   107	                c.AgentPrometheusPort = wellknownports.CiliumPrometheusPort
   108	        }
   109	
   110	        if c.IPAM == "" {
   111	                c.IPAM = "kubernetes"
   112	        }
   113	
   114	        if c.Masquerade == nil {
   115	                c.Masquerade = fi.PtrTo(!clusterSpec.IsIPv6Only())
   116	        }
   117	
   118	        if c.Tunnel == "" {
   119	                if c.IPAM == "eni" || clusterSpec.IsIPv6Only() {
   120	                        c.Tunnel = "disabled"
   121	                } else {
   122	                        c.Tunnel = "vxlan"
   123	                }
   124	        }
   125	
   126	        if c.EnableRemoteNodeIdentity == nil {
   127	                c.EnableRemoteNodeIdentity = fi.PtrTo(true)
   128	        }
   129	
   130	        if c.EnableUnreachableRoutes == nil {
   131	                c.EnableUnreachableRoutes = fi.PtrTo(false)
   132	        }
   133	
   134	        if c.EnableBPFMasquerade == nil {
   135	                c.EnableBPFMasquerade = fi.PtrTo(c.IPAM == "eni")
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        if c.EnableL7Proxy == nil {
   139	                c.EnableL7Proxy = fi.PtrTo(true)
   140	        }
   141	
   142	        if c.EnableLocalRedirectPolicy == nil {
   143	                c.EnableLocalRedirectPolicy = fi.PtrTo(false)
   144	        }
   145	
   146	        if c.DisableCNPStatusUpdates == nil {
   147	                c.DisableCNPStatusUpdates = fi.PtrTo(true)
   148	        }
   149	
   150	        if c.CPURequest == nil {
   151	                defaultCPURequest := resource.MustParse("25m")
   152	                c.CPURequest = &defaultCPURequest
   153	        }
   154	
   155	        if c.MemoryRequest == nil {
   156	                defaultMemoryRequest := resource.MustParse("128Mi")
   157	                c.MemoryRequest = &defaultMemoryRequest
   158	        }
   159	
   160	        if c.EnableEncryption && c.EncryptionType == "" {
   161	                c.EncryptionType = kops.CiliumEncryptionTypeIPSec
   162	        }
   163	
   164	        if c.CniExclusive == nil {
   165	                c.CniExclusive = fi.PtrTo(true)
   166	        }
   167	
   168	        hubble := c.Hubble
   169	        if hubble != nil {
   170	                if hubble.Enabled == nil {
   171	                        hubble.Enabled = fi.PtrTo(true)
   172	                }
   173	        } else {
   174	                c.Hubble = &kops.HubbleSpec{
   175	                        Enabled: fi.PtrTo(false),
   176	                }
   177	        }
   178	
   179	        ingress := c.Ingress
   180	        if ingress != nil {
   181	                if ingress.Enabled == nil {
   182	                        ingress.Enabled = fi.PtrTo(true)
   183	                }
   184	        } else {
   185	                c.Ingress = &kops.CiliumIngressSpec{
   186	                        Enabled: fi.PtrTo(false),
   187	                }
   188	        }
   189	
   190	        gatewayAPI := c.GatewayAPI
   191	        if gatewayAPI != nil {
   192	                if gatewayAPI.Enabled == nil {
   193	                        gatewayAPI.Enabled = fi.PtrTo(true)
   194	                }
   195	        } else {
   196	                c.GatewayAPI = &kops.CiliumGatewayAPISpec{
   197	                        Enabled: fi.PtrTo(false),
   198	                }
   199	        }
   200	
   201	        return nil
   202	}

    26	        f := NewClusterField(fieldPath)
    27	        return f.HumanPath()
    28	}

    32	        f := NewClusterField(fieldPath)
    33	        return f.InternalPath()
    34	}

    58	func (f *ClusterField) PathInV1Alpha2() string {

    60	                if mapping.V1Alpha3 == f.Path {

    62	                }

    72	                }
    73	        }
